cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.4)

# Hunter package manager setup
include("cmake/HunterGate.cmake")
HunterGate(
    URL "https://github.com/cpp-pm/hunter/archive/v0.23.251.tar.gz"
    SHA1 "5659b15dc0884d4b03dbd95710e6a1fa0fc3258d"
)

# Project settings
project(print)
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD 11)
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD_REQUIRED ON)

# Version information
set(PRINT_VERSION_MAJOR 0)
set(PRINT_VERSION_MINOR 1)
set(PRINT_VERSION_PATCH 0)
set(PRINT_VERSION_TWEAK 0)
set(PRINT_VERSION
  ${PRINT_VERSION_MAJOR}.${PRINT_VERSION_MINOR}.${PRINT_VERSION_PATCH}.${PRINT_VERSION_TWEAK})
set(PRINT_VERSION_STRING "v${PRINT_VERSION}")

# Options
option(BUILD_EXAMPLES "Build examples" OFF)
option(BUILD_TESTS "Build tests" OFF)

# Library target
add_library(print STATIC ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/sources/print.cpp)

target_include_directories(print PUBLIC
  $<BUILD_INTERFACE:${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/include>
  $<INSTALL_INTERFACE:include>
)

# Examples
if(BUILD_EXAMPLES)
  file(GLOB EXAMPLE_SOURCES "${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/examples/*.cpp")
  foreach(EXAMPLE_SOURCE ${EXAMPLE_SOURCES})
    get_filename_component(EXAMPLE_NAME ${EXAMPLE_SOURCE} NAME_WE)
    add_executable(${EXAMPLE_NAME} ${EXAMPLE_SOURCE})
    target_link_libraries(${EXAMPLE_NAME} print)
    install(TARGETS ${EXAMPLE_NAME}
      RUNTIME DESTINATION bin
    )
  endforeach()
endif()

# Installation
install(TARGETS print
    EXPORT print-config
    ARCHIVE DESTINATION lib
    LIBRARY DESTINATION lib
)

install(DIRECTORY ${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/include/ DESTINATION include)
install(EXPORT print-config DESTINATION cmake)

# CPack configuration
include(InstallRequiredSystemLibraries)
set(CPACK_PACKAGE_NAME "print")
set(CPACK_PACKAGE_VERSION "${PRINT_VERSION}")
set(CPACK_PACKAGE_CONTACT "Your Name <your.email@example.com>")
set(CPACK_PACKAGE_DESCRIPTION "A simple printing library")
EOFif()est(NAME check COMMAND check)GTest::GTest GTest::Main)

TEST(PrintTest, BasicTest) {
    std::ostringstream oss;
    print("test", oss);
    EXPECT_EQ(oss.str(), "test\n");
}

TEST(PrintTest, DefaultStreamTest) {
    testing::internal::CaptureStdout();
    print("default");
    std::string output = testing::internal::GetCapturedStdout();
    EXPECT_EQ(output, "default\n");
}
EOF

if(HUNTER_GTest_VERSION VERSION_LESS 1.8.0 OR HUNTER_GTest_VERSION VERSION_GREATER_EQUAL 1.11.0)
  set(_gtest_license "LICENSE")

  set(_gtest_license "googletest/LICENSE")
endif()

# gtest_force_shared_crt prevents GoogleTest from modifying options
# rather than forcing it to use shared libraries
hunter_cmake_args(
    GTest
    CMAKE_ARGS
    HUNTER_INSTALL_LICENSE_FILES=${_gtest_license}
    gtest_force_shared_crt=TRUE
)

hunter_cacheable(GTest)
hunter_download(PACKAGE_NAME GTest PACKAGE_INTERNAL_DEPS_ID 1)
